Enclosing class:
[ProfileImplementation](ProfileImplementation.html)

@OpenApipublic abstract static classProfileImplementation.StereotypeWrapper
extends [Object](https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/17/docs/api/java.base/java/lang/Object.html)

Base class for generated stereotype wrapper for Stereotype from a modeled Profile (UML).
 Generated stereotype wrapper provides convenience methods for applying / un-applying stereotype to given element,
 manipulating tagged value values.

<div class="type-signature"><span class="annotations">@OpenApi
</span><span class="modifiers">public abstract static class </span><span class="element-name type-name-label">ProfileImplementation.StereotypeWrapper</span>
<span class="extends-implements">extends <a class="external-link" href="https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/17/docs/api/java.base/java/lang/Object.html" title="class or interface in java.lang">Object</a></span></div>
<div class="block">Base class for generated stereotype wrapper for Stereotype from a modeled Profile (UML).
 Generated stereotype wrapper provides convenience methods for applying / un-applying stereotype to given element,
 manipulating tagged value values.</div>
</section>
